***thong.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a> (72455)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">thwong</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">thwang</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þwong</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þwang</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þweng</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þwæng</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a>, strap, cord, strip of leather; phylactery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þwangiz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þwanguz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">coercion, constraint, <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a>, clamp, strap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*twenk-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to squeeze, press, pressure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">thwang</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">thwayng</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">thang</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">dwenge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clamp, <a href = vnd.unilang:jaws.html>jaws</a>, steel-trap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zwinge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vise, clamp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">tveng</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shoestrap, shoelace</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">þvengur</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strap, <a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a>, latchet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thongs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A strip of leather.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the plural<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An item of footwear, usually of rubber, secured by two straps which join to pass between the big <a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a> and its neighbour.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1963</b> March 16,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hal_Porter" class="extiw" title="w:Hal Porter"><a href = vnd.unilang:hal.html>Hal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>Porter</a></a>,  “Little old lady passing by”, in  <cite>The Bulletin</cite>, page 22, column 3:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Because of August he wears <a href = vnd.unilang:shorts.html>shorts</a> and sandals, the Japanese <i>geta</i> sort called <b>thongs</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1964</b>, The Beach Boys, <i>All Summer Long</i>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:t-shirts.html>T-shirts</a>, cut-offs, and a pair of thongs (<a href = vnd.unilang:t-shirts.html>T-shirts</a>, cut-offs, and a pair of thongs).</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2006</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> Murray, David Poole, Grant Jones, <i>Contemporary Issues in Management and Organisational Behaviour</i>, Thomson, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=B3jLCYTl8GICamp;pg=PA106amp;lpg=PA106amp;dq=%22thong%22%7C%22thongs%22+australia+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;source=blamp;ots=TG3xwcFguHamp;sig=0GRl0y-_iiNIIUlYrGLZptufxN4amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=NH2CUPrqAa-ViAesh4DgDQamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22thong%22%7C%22thongs%22%20australia%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 108</a>,
<dl><dd>Players <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> up for questioning wearing <b>thongs</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:shorts.html>shorts</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:t-shirts.html>T-shirts</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:steve.html>Steve</a> Parish,  <cite>Eccentric Australia</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=3ObAXLQU9Y4Camp;pg=PA104amp;lpg=PA104amp;dq=%22thong%22%7C%22thongs%22+australia+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;source=blamp;ots=fCARBBKASSamp;sig=HuTN3MAcq81MMKoJGoAr5W1wFpEamp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=NH2CUPrqAa-ViAesh4DgDQamp;redir_esc=y">[1]</a></sup>, page 104:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Thongs are the favoured footwear for many Aussies, especially near the <a href = vnd.unilang:beaches.html>beaches</a>, but most people in the <a href = vnd.unilang:outback.html>Outback</a> find that they can′t put a foot wrong with a tough, nicely worn-in pair or workboots.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2009</b>, Charles Rawlings-Way, <i>Sydney</i>, Lonely Planet, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=lefJBm4Jk7cCamp;pg=PA126amp;lpg=PA126amp;dq=%22thong%22%7C%22thongs%22+australia+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;source=blamp;ots=M5OMVHwoHWamp;sig=DJX1gA76W7xi3F1E0RhluL7PHSQamp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=NH2CUPrqAa-ViAesh4DgDQamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22thong%22%7C%22thongs%22%20australia%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 126</a>,
<dl><dd>You shouldn′t face condescension if you rock into a boutique in your thongs and a singlet, but neither will you be treated like a princess just because you′ve splashed $5000 on daddy′s credit card.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An undergarment or swimwear consisting of very narrow <a href = vnd.unilang:strips.html>strips</a> designed to cover just the genitals and nothing more.
<dl><dd><i>No! I <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> buy you a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thong.html>thong</a></b>. You're too young for that.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>The largest section of a bullwhip constructed of many straps of braided leather.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">an item of footwear</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <i>see list in</i> <b><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:flip-flop.html>flip-flop</a></span></b></li>

</body> 
***thor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thor.html>thor</a> (16766)</h1><br></body> 
***thorax.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thorax.html>thorax</a> (58976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:thorax.html>thorax</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θώραξ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">thṓrax</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a breastplate, cuirass, corslet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thorax.html>thorax</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thoraces</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thoraxes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The region of the mammalian body between the neck and abdomen as well as the cavity containing the heart and lungs.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology and arachnology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The middle of three distinct divisions in an insect, crustacean or arachnid body to which the <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> are attached.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="4" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">thoracal</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">thoracic</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">thoracic vertebra</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">thoracoplasty</span></li></ul></div><div class="list-switcher-element" data-showtext=" show more ▼ " data-hidetext=" show less  " style="display: none;"> </div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:thorax.html>thorax</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:anatomie.html>anatomie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:borstkas.html>borstkas</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ribbenkast.html>ribbenkast</a>, borstholte</li></ol>
</body>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thunderbolt.html>thunderbolt</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thunderbolts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A flash of lightning accompanied by a crash of thunder.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An event that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> terrible, horrific or unexpected.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1697</b>,  “<span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(please specify the book number)</span>”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="w:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>, transl., <cite>The Works of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virgil" class="extiw" title="w:Virgil"><a href = vnd.unilang:virgil.html>Virgil</a></a>: Containing His Pastorals, Georgics, and Æneis.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Translated into English Verse; by Mr. DRYDEN. Adorn’d with a Hundred Sculptures.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, London |  Printed for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacob_Tonson" class="extiw" title="w:Jacob Tonson"><a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> Tonson</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Judges Head in Fleetstreet, near the Inner-Temple-Gate.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/403869432">403869432</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>the Scipios' worth, those <b>thunderbolts</b> of war</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Vehement threatening or censure; especially, ecclesiastical denunciation; fulmination.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Hakewill and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>He severely threatens such with the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thunderbolt.html>thunderbolt</a></b> of excommunication.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">soccer</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A very powerful shot.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> February 5,  Michael Kevin Darling,  “Tottenham 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 1 Bolton”, in  <cite>BBC</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/eng_prem/9382905.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Substitute <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Niko_Kranjcar" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Niko Kranjcar"><a href = vnd.unilang:niko.html>Niko</a> Kranjcar</a>'s injury-time <b><a href = vnd.unilang:thunderbolt.html>thunderbolt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> Tottenham a dramatic win <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> Bolton.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">paleontology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A belemnite, or thunderstone.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A charge in the form of two joined bundles with four <a href = vnd.unilang:rays.html>rays</a> of lightning emerging from them, resembling the <a href = vnd.unilang:thunderbolt.html>thunderbolt</a> of Jupiter.</li>
<li>A daring or irresistible hero.</li></ol>

***thwaite.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:thwaite.html>thwaite</a> (62699)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*thwait</i>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">þveit</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">paddock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">þveita</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hurl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">whittle</i>), Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">døjt</i> (“<small><sup>1</sup><big>⁄</big><sub>160</sub></small> of the gulden”, dialectal: “a small coin”), German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Deut</i>, Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duit.html>duit</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þwītan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to thwite; cut; cut off</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">doit</i>, and possibly of <i><span class="Latn" lang="en">twat</span></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:thwaite.html>thwaite</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">thwaites</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of forest <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> cleared for agriculture or habitation; a clearing; assart</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">thwite</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">twaite</i></span></span></li></ol>

***tic.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tic.html>tic</a> (21213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:tic.html>tic</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tic.html>tic</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tics.html>tics</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A sudden, nonrhythmic <a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a> movement or vocalization.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> done or produced habitually or characteristically.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b> January 19,  <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> Bradshaw,  “T2 Trainspotting review – choose a sequel that doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> disappoint”, in  <cite>the Guardian</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.theguardian.com/film/2017/jan/19/t2-trainspotting-review-ewan-mcgregor-danny-boyle-sequel">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Boyle revives some of the stylistic <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tics.html>tics</a></b> which found themselves being ripped off by geezer-gangster Britflicks back in the day, but now the freezeframes are briefer, sharper; the movie itself refers back to the original with variant flashback versions of famous <a href = vnd.unilang:scenes.html>scenes</a>, but also <a href = vnd.unilang:super.html>Super</a> 8-type images of the boys’ poignant boyhood in primary school.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">abbreviation<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ticket</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tic.html>tic</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tics.html>tics</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ticcing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ticced</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To exhibit a <a href = vnd.unilang:tic.html>tic</a>; to undergo a sudden, semi-voluntary muscle movement.</li></ol>

***tief.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a> (87359)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">tiuf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">tiuf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*deupaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰewb-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">deep</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diep.html>diep</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deep</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">dyb</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">dyp</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">djúpur</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de">tiefer</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am tiefsten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deep (also figuratively)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a></b> ist <a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>das</a> Wasser?</i>
<dl><dd>How deep <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the water?</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:sie.html>Sie</a> hat ein <b>tiefes</b> Verständnis <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> russischen Kultur.</i>
<dl><dd>She <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a deep understanding of Russian culture.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>low
<dl><dd><i>Du hast <a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>das</a> Bild zu <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>tief</a></b> gehängt.</i>
<dl><dd>You hung the picture too low.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">niedrig</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a more generally applicable translation of English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">low</i>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tief.html>Tief</a></i> can cover the meaning of <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">niedrig</i> in many contexts, but not vice versa.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="de">vertiefen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="de">knietief</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="de">Tiefschlag</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="de">Tiefsee</span></li></ul>
</body>

***tierelantijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tierelantijn.html>tierelantijn</a> (98764)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Expansion of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tieretein</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fabric made of wool and cotton</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tierelantijn.html>tierelantijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tierelantijnen.html>tierelantijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tierelantijn.html>tierelantijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly plural<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A flourish, something ornamental and not functional.</li></ol>

***tieren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tieren.html>tieren</a> (36571)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tieren.html>tieren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*tiari-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">neat, splendid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*DiH-or-i-</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>  The ultimate origin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> uncertain, but cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">tærr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clear (water)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which could be related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">tár</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> lt;lt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tahrą</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zieren</i>, and also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sieren.html>sieren</a></i> which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed from Middle High German.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tieren.html>tieren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to thrive, prosper</li>
<li>to make a fuss, to rant</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Titte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nipple; breast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*titt-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">teat; nipple; breast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tata-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">father; parent; nipple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zitze</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tit</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">teat</i>.

***tijdstip.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijdstip.html>tijdstip</a> (4492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stip.html>stip</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijdstip.html>tijdstip</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijdstippen.html>tijdstippen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijdstip.html>tijdstipje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> in time, point in time, time of day.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tijdstip.html>tijdstip</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:sliep.html>sliep</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> still sleeping at that <b>time</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondanks.html>Ondanks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> late <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tijdstip.html>tijdstip</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:druk.html>druk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straat.html>straat</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Despite the late <b>hour</b> the streets <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> still very crowded.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vak.html>vak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">section, compartment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tijtverdrijf</i>. ***tikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tikken.html>tikken</a> (11921)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tikken.html>tikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tick, to make a ticking sound</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tap</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to type on a typewriter or keyboard</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tag (in a children's game)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">type</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:typen.html>typen</a></span></li></ul>

***tiller.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a> (87337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">tilier</i>; equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">till</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tillers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person who tills; a farmer.
<ul><li><b>2000</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alasdair_Gray" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alasdair Gray">Alasdair Gray</a>, <i>The Book of Prefaces</i>, Bloomsbury 2002, page 63:
<dl><dd>In France, Europe's most fertile and cultivated <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, the <b>tillers</b> of it suffered more and more hunger.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A machine that mechanically tills the soil.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">machine</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">cultivator</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>Tiller</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Tillerson</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*tilȝer, *telȝer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">telgor</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">telgra</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">telgre</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"twig, branch, shoot"</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> (also <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">telga</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">telge</i> (whence <span class="Latn" lang="en">tillow</span>)), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*telgô</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*telgǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*telguz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twig, branch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*delgʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to split, divide, cut, carve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:telg.html>telg</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">descendant, scion, offshoot, shoot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_Low_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch Low Saxon">Dutch Low Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-nl">telge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twig, branch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zelge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twig, branch, bough</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">telning</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">branch, scion, sapling</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">tág</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">willow-twig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tillers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A young tree.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Evelyn to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A shoot of a plant which springs from the root or bottom of the original stalk; a sapling; a sucker.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">tillers</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tillering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">tillered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To produce new shoots from the root or from around the bottom of the original stalk; stool.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">telier</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beam used in weaving</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">telarium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tēla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">web</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tillers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archery</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The stock; a beam on a <a href = vnd.unilang:crossbow.html>crossbow</a> carved to fit the arrow, or the point of balance in a longbow.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1608–1610</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Beaumont" class="extiw" title="w:Francis Beaumont">Francis Beaumont</a> |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Fletcher_(playwright)" class="extiw" title="w:John Fletcher (playwright)">John <a href = vnd.unilang:fletcher.html>Fletcher</a></a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philaster_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Philaster (play)">Philaster: Or, Love Lies a Bleeding</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beaumont_and_Fletcher_folios" class="extiw" title="w:Beaumont and Fletcher folios">Comedies and <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Written by Francis Beavmont and Iohn Fletcher Gentlemen. Never Printed before, and Now Published by the Authours Originall Copies.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, London |  Printed for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Robinson" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Robinson">Humphrey Robinson</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Three Pidgeons">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, and for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Moseley" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Moseley">Humphrey Moseley</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Princes Armes in St Pauls Church-yard.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, published 1679, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/3083972">3083972</a></small>, Act 2, scene 2:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>You can shoot in a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a> of iron or wood connected with the rudderhead and leadline, usually forward, in which the rudder <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> moved as desired by the <a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a> (FM 55-501).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The handle of the rudder which the helmsman holds to steer the boat, a piece of wood or metal extending forward from the rudder <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> or through the transom. Generally attached at the top of the rudder.</li>
<li>A handle; a stalk.</li>
<li>The rear-wheel steering control, aboard a <a href = vnd.unilang:tiller.html>tiller</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:truck.html>truck</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A small drawer; a till.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Dryden to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***timbre.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a> (58960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τύμπανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">túmpanon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">drum</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tympanum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/timbre" class="extiw" title="w:timbre"><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/timbre" class="extiw" title="w:timbre">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">timbres</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The quality of a sound independent of its pitch and volume.
<ul><li><b>1931</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H._P._Lovecraft" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:H. P. Lovecraft">H. P. Lovecraft</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Whisperer_in_Darkness" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Whisperer in Darkness">The Whisperer in Darkness</a></i>, chapter 7:
<dl><dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a hard whisper to catch at first, since the grey moustache concealed all movements of the <a href = vnd.unilang:lips.html>lips</a>, and something in its <b><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></b> disturbed <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> greatly; but by concentrating my attention I could soon make out its purport surprisingly well.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The pitch of a sound as <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> by the ear, described relative to its absolute pitch.
<ul><li><dl><dd>When someone speaks after inhaling helium, their voice <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></b>. With sulfur hexafluoride, the result <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a lower <b><a href = vnd.unilang:timbre.html>timbre</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The crest on a coat of arms.</li></ol>
